MARION HALE BRITTEN AND MRS. IDA S. CHADWICK 1930 GENERAL INDEX AMERICAN ANTHROPOLOGIST CURRENT ANTHROPOLOGICAL LITERATURE AND MEMOIRS OF THE AMERICAN ANTHROPOLOGICAL ASSOCIATION 1888-1928 ALFRED VINCENT KIDDER WITH THE AID OF MRS. MARION HALE BRITTEN AND MRS. IDA S. CHADWICK</page><page sequence="2">w PREFACE The American Anthropologist has been published in two series. The first or old series of eleven volumes was published under the auspices of the Anthropological Society of Washington during the years 188^-1898 inclusive. In this index the old series is indicated by a capital "0" pre ceding the volume number; thus "04:25" means "Old Series, volume 4, page 25." With the founding of the American Anthropological Association, the American Anthropologist became the official organ of that organiza tion, the Anthropological Society of Washington, and the American Ethnological Society of New York. A new series began with the volume for 1899-. This index covers the first thirty volumes of the new series; In this index the volume number without a preceding letter indicates' new series; thus, "21:41" means New Series, volume 21, page 41. The Memoirs of the American Anthropological Association, a series of papers issued at irregular intervals, are indicated in this index by "mem." preceding the volume number or the memoir number. The first 28 memoirs were published in six volumes. Subsequent memoirs were issued with separate pagination and not in volumes. Examples of cita tions are mem., IV, no. 4, and mem. no. 32, which are to be read as Memoirs, volume IV, no. 4 and Memoirs, no. 32. A third publication, issued jointly by the American Anthropological Association and the American Folk-Lore Society, was Current Anthro pological Literature. Only two volumes were issued, dated 1912 and 1913. These are cited in the index as C.A.L. 1 and C.A.L. 2, followed by the page reference. The publication of this index has been made possible by a generous grant from the Carnegie Corporation of New York to the Council of Learned Societies.</page><page sequence="3">TABLE OF CONTENTS Authors of Original Articles 1 Authors of Reviews 48 Authors of Works Reviewed 83 Subject Index 117 Obituaries 192</page><page sequence="4">AUTHORS OF ORIGINAL ARTICLES Adler, C., Oriental customs of cour- Babcock, W.
